  {
    sembol: "Tarih",
    degisim: "Emeklilik Fonları",
    sonToplamYuzde: "Yatırım Fonları",
    ilkToplamYuzde: "Toplam",
    sonToplamTakasTl: "Fiyat",
    ilkToplamTakasTl: null,
    takasTlSonEmeklilikFon: null,
    yuzdeSonEmeklilikFon: null,

    takasTlSonYatirimFon: null,
    yuzdeSonYatirimFon: null,
    takasTlIlkYatirimFon: null,
    yuzdeIlkYatirimFon: null
  },
  
];

type SortKey =
  | "sembol"
  | "degisim"
  | "sonToplamYuzde"
  | "ilkToplamYuzde"
  | "sonToplamTakasTl"
  | "ilkToplamTakasTl"
  | "takasTlSonEmeklilikFon"
  | "yuzdeSonEmeklilikFon"
  | "takasTlIlkEmeklilikFon"
  | "yuzdeIlkEmeklilikFon"
  | "takasTlSonYatirimFon"
  | "yuzdeSonYatirimFon"
  | "takasTlIlkYatirimFon"
  | "yuzdeIlkYatirimFon";

const columns: { key: SortKey; label: string; align?: "left" | "right" }[] = [
  { key: "sembol", label: "Sembol", align: "left" },
  { key: "degisim", label: "Değişim", align: "right" },
  { key: "sonToplamYuzde", label: "Son Toplam %", align: "right" },
  { key: "ilkToplamYuzde", label: "İlk Toplam %", align: "right" },
  { key: "sonToplamTakasTl", label: "Son Toplam Takas TL", align: "right" },
  { key: "ilkToplamTakasTl", label: "İlk Toplam Takas TL", align: "right" },
  { key: "takasTlSonEmeklilikFon", label: "Takas TL Son (Emeklilik Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "yuzdeSonEmeklilikFon", label: "% Son (Emeklilik Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "takasTlIlkEmeklilikFon", label: "Takas TL İlk (Emeklilik Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "yuzdeIlkEmeklilikFon", label: "% İlk (Emeklilik Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "takasTlSonYatirimFon", label: "Takas TL Son (Yatırım Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "yuzdeSonYatirimFon", label: "% Son (Yatırım Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "takasTlIlkYatirimFon", label: "Takas TL İlk (Yatırım Fon)", align: "right" },
  { key: "yuzdeIlkYatirimFon", label: "% İlk (Yatırım Fon)", align: "right" },
];

function parsePercent(value: string | number | null) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") return -Infinity;
  if (typeof value === "number") return value;

  const normalized = value.replace("%", "").replace(",", ".").trim();
  const number = Number(normalized);
  return Number.isNaN(number) ? -Infinity : number;
}

function formatTl(value: number | null) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return "-";
  return new Intl.NumberFormat("tr-TR").format(value);
}

function formatText(value: string | number | null) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") return "-";
  return String(value);
}

export default function HaftalikFonTercihleriPage() {
  const [sortKey, setSortKey] = useState<SortKey>("degisim");
  const [sortDirection, setSortDirection] = useState<"asc" | "desc">("desc");
  const tableScrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
  const stickyScrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
  const stickyScrollContentRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);

  const handleSort = (key: SortKey) => {
    if (sortKey === key) {
      setSortDirection((prev) => (prev === "asc" ? "desc" : "asc"));
      return;
    }

    setSortKey(key);
    setSortDirection(key === "sembol" ? "asc" : "desc");
  };


  useEffect(() => {
    const tableEl = tableScrollRef.current;
    const stickyEl = stickyScrollRef.current;
    const stickyContentEl = stickyScrollContentRef.current;

    if (!tableEl || !stickyEl || !stickyContentEl) return;

    const syncWidths = () => {
      const table = tableEl.querySelector("table");
      const tableWidth = table instanceof HTMLElement ? table.scrollWidth : tableEl.scrollWidth;
      stickyContentEl.style.width = `${tableWidth}px`;
    };

    let isSyncingFromTable = false;
    let isSyncingFromSticky = false;

    const handleTableScroll = () => {
      if (!stickyEl || isSyncingFromSticky) return;
      isSyncingFromTable = true;
      stickyEl.scrollLeft = tableEl.scrollLeft;
      isSyncingFromTable = false;
    };

    const handleStickyScroll = () => {
      if (!tableEl || isSyncingFromTable) return;
      isSyncingFromSticky = true;
      tableEl.scrollLeft = stickyEl.scrollLeft;
      isSyncingFromSticky = false;
    };

    syncWidths();
    stickyEl.scrollLeft = tableEl.scrollLeft;

    tableEl.addEventListener("scroll", handleTableScroll);
    stickyEl.addEventListener("scroll", handleStickyScroll);
    window.addEventListener("resize", syncWidths);

    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(syncWidths);
    resizeObserver.observe(tableEl);

    return () => {
      tableEl.removeEventListener("scroll", handleTableScroll);
      stickyEl.removeEventListener("scroll", handleStickyScroll);
      window.removeEventListener("resize", syncWidths);
      resizeObserver.disconnect();
    };
  }, []);

  const sortedData = useMemo(() => {
    const data = [...fonVerileri];

    data.sort((a, b) => {
      const aValue = a[sortKey];
      const bValue = b[sortKey];

      let comparison = 0;

      if (sortKey === "sembol") {
        comparison = String(aValue ?? "").localeCompare(String(bValue ?? ""), "tr");
      } else if (
        sortKey === "degisim" ||
        sortKey === "sonToplamYuzde" ||
        sortKey === "ilkToplamYuzde" ||
        sortKey === "yuzdeSonEmeklilikFon" ||
        sortKey === "yuzdeIlkEmeklilikFon" ||
        sortKey === "yuzdeSonYatirimFon" ||
        sortKey === "yuzdeIlkYatirimFon"
      ) {
        comparison = parsePercent(aValue as string | null) - parsePercent(bValue as string | null);
      } else {
        comparison = Number(aValue ?? -Infinity) - Number(bValue ?? -Infinity);
      }

      return sortDirection === "asc" ? comparison : -comparison;
    });

    return data;
  }, [sortDirection, sortKey]);

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-white px-4 py-6 md:px-6">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-[1600px]">
        <div className="mb-6 flex gap-3">
          <Link
            href="/"
            className="inline-block rounded-xl border border-zinc-300 bg-white px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-700 hover:bg-zinc-100"
          >
            Ana Sayfa
          </Link>

          <Link
            href="/fonlar"
            className="inline-block rounded-xl border border-zinc-300 bg-white px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-700 hover:bg-zinc-100"
          >
            Geri
          </Link>
        </div>

        <h1 className="mb-2 text-3xl font-bold text-zinc-900">
          Haftalık Yatırım Fonlarının En Çok Tercih Ettiği Hisseler
        </h1>

        <p className="mb-6 text-sm text-zinc-600">
          Sütun başlıklarına tıklayarak artan ve azalan sıralama yapabilirsin.
        </p>

        <div className="rounded-2xl border border-zinc-200 bg-white">
          <div
            ref={tableScrollRef}
            className="w-full overflow-x-auto pb-2 [scrollbar-width:none] [&::-webkit-scrollbar]:hidden"
          >
            <div className="inline-block min-w-full align-top">
              <table className="min-w-[1900px] border-collapse text-sm whitespace-nowrap">
              <thead className="bg-zinc-100">
                <tr>
                  {columns.map((column) => {
                    const isActive = sortKey === column.key;
                    const arrow = isActive ? (sortDirection === "asc" ? "▲" : "▼") : "↕";

                    return (
                      <th
                        key={column.key}
                        className={`border-b border-zinc-200 px-4 py-3 ${column.align === "right" ? "text-right" : "text-left"}`}
                      >
                        <button
                          type="button"
                          onClick={() => handleSort(column.key)}
                          className="flex w-full items-center gap-2 font-semibold text-zinc-800"
                        >
                          <span className={column.align === "right" ? "ml-auto" : ""}>
                            {column.label}
                          </span>
                          <span className="text-xs text-zinc-500">{arrow}</span>
                        </button>
                      </th>
                    );
                  })}
                </tr>
              </thead>

              <tbody>
                {sortedData.map((item, index) => (
                  <tr
                    key={`${item.sembol}-${index}`}
                    className={index % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-sky-50"}
                  >
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 font-semibold text-zinc-900">
                      {formatText(item.sembol)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.degisim)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.sonToplamYuzde)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.ilkToplamYuzde)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatTl(item.sonToplamTakasTl)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatTl(item.ilkToplamTakasTl)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatTl(item.takasTlSonEmeklilikFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.yuzdeSonEmeklilikFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatTl(item.takasTlIlkEmeklilikFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.yuzdeIlkEmeklilikFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatTl(item.takasTlSonYatirimFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.yuzdeSonYatirimFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatTl(item.takasTlIlkYatirimFon)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="border-b border-zinc-100 px-4 py-3 text-right text-zinc-700">
                      {formatText(item.yuzdeIlkYatirimFon)}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="sticky bottom-0 z-30 mt-3 bg-white/95 pb-1 pt-1 backdrop-blur">
          <div
            ref={stickyScrollRef}
            className="overflow-x-auto rounded-full border border-zinc-200 bg-zinc-100 [scrollbar-width:thin]"
          >
            <div ref={stickyScrollContentRef} className="h-4" />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}
